# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="b3b42-103">Microsoft 365 de criptografia</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b3b42-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b3b42-104">Microsoft 365 aproveita vários provedores de certificados diferentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b3b42-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b3b42-105">A seguir descreve a lista completa de certificados Microsoft 365 raiz conhecidos que os clientes podem encontrar ao acessar Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b3b42-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b3b42-106">Para obter informações sobre os certificados que você pode precisar instalar em sua própria infraestrutura, consulte [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b3b42-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b3b42-107">As informações de certificado a seguir se aplicam a todas as instâncias de nuvem nacionais e mundiais de Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b3b42-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>
